***стриженый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стриженый.html>стри́женый</a> (11392)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стричь.html>стричь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stričʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-еный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-enyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стриженый.html>стри́женый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stríženyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>short-haired, <i>(sheep)</i> shorn, <i>(hair)</i> short</li>
<li><i>(trees)</i> clipped, <i>(grass)</i> mown</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Short forms <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стриженый.html>стри́жен</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:стриженый.html>стри́жена</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:стриженый.html>стри́жено</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:стриженый.html>стри́жены</a></span> theoretically exist, but are usually avoided due to their similarity to short forms of the past passive participle of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стричь.html>стричь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stričʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>

***стриптиз.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стриптиз.html>стрипти́з</a> (20456)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">striptease</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стриптиз.html>стрипти́з</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">striptíz</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стриптиз.html>стрипти́за</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>striptease</li></ol>

***стричь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стричь.html>стричь</a> (7370)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*striťi</i>, from earlier <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*strigti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стричь.html>стричь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stričʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:остричь.html>остри́чь</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постричь.html>постри́чь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cut (hair, fur, grass, etc.), to shear, to clip, to trim
<ul><li><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white">Андрей <a href = vnd.unilang:белый.html>Белый</a>, <i>Петербург</i> 1913-1914:<dl><dd><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:засунуть.html>засу́нул</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:карман.html>карма́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:миниатюрный.html>миниатю́рные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ножницы.html>но́жницы</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рыми</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:наверное.html>наве́рное</a>, франтик <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:утро.html>утрам</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стричь.html>стрижёт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ноготь.html>но́гти</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> ― <a href = vnd.unilang:броситься.html>бро́сился</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on zasúnul v karmán miniatjúrnyje nóžnicy, kotórymi, navérnoje, frantik po utram <b>strižót</b> nógti, i ― brósilsja</i></dd><dd>he slipped in his pocket (a pair) of miniature scissors with which, probably, the dandy <b>cut</b> his nails in the morning, and ran away</dd></dl></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стричься.html>стри́чься</a> (25030)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стричь.html>стри́чь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stríčʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стричься.html>стри́чься</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stríčʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">остри́чься</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">обстри́чься</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cut one's hair, to get a haircut</li>
<li>to wear one's hair trimmed <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in a specified way</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стричь.html>стри́чь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stríčʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***строгать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:строгать.html>строга́ть</a> (24599)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">стръгати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">strŭgati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*strъgati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:строгать.html>строга́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">strogátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to plane, to shave <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in terms of wood</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to slice</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:строевой.html>строево́й</a> (9220)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">стро́(ить)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stró(itʹ)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ево́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-evój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:строевой.html>строево́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">strojevój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> drill
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:строевой.html>строево́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шаг.html>шаг</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>strojevój</b> šag</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>drill</b> step</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> frontline

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> construction</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> building
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:строевой.html>строево́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>strojevój</b> les</i> ― <span class="e-translation">timber</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>building</b> lumber</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:строжайший.html>строжа́йший</a> (14715)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***строить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>строи́ть</a> (1519)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">строити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stroiti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*strojiti</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*strojь</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>стро́ить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stróitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:построить.html>постро́ить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to build, to construct
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>стро́ить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:воздушный.html>возду́шные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:замок.html>за́мки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stróitʹ</b> vozdúšnyje zámki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to build castles in the air</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to make, to construct
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>стро́ить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:фраза.html>фра́зу</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:предложение.html>предложе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stróitʹ</b> frázu/predložénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to construct a sentence</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>стро́ить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:графика.html>гра́фик</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stróitʹ</b> gráfik</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to draw a graph</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>стро́ить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:треугольник.html>треуго́льник</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stróitʹ</b> treugólʹnik</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to construct a triangle</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>стро́ить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:угол.html>у́гол</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stróitʹ</b> úgol</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to plot an angle</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>стро́ить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stróitʹ</b> iz sebjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to try to appear <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">as</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, pose <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">as</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>стро́ить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:козни.html>ко́зни</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stróitʹ</b> kózni</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to scheme, to plot</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>стро́ить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:план.html>пла́ны</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stróitʹ</b> plány</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make plans</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>стро́ить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рожа.html>ро́жи</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stróitʹ</b> róži</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make faces</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to form, to draw up, to dress up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>стро́ить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:колонна.html>коло́нну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stróitʹ</b> v kolónnu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to form in column</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:троить.html>трои́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">troítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>строи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stroítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:троить.html>трои́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">стра́ивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to connect (string, yarn, etc.) in three strands</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to strike three items</li>
<li>to plough (a field) for the third time</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:строиться.html>стро́иться</a> (4829)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>стро́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stróitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:строиться.html>стро́иться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stróitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:построиться.html>постро́иться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be built, to be under construction</li>
<li>to build a house for oneself</li>
<li>to draw up, to form, to assume formation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:строиться.html>стро́йся</a>!</b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>strójsja!</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">fall in!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>стро́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stróitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***строй.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>строй</a> (1729)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>строи</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stroi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*strojь</i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>строи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stroitʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to build, construct</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>строй</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stroj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>стро́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>стро́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:строй.html>стро́ев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>order, array</li>
<li>line</li>
<li>system, order, regime</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tune</li></ol>

***стройка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стройка.html>стро́йка</a> (5504)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">стройи</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stroji</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*strew-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to strew, to spread out</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стройка.html>стро́йка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">strójka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стройка.html>стро́йки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стройка.html>стро́йки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стройка.html>стро́ек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>building, construction</li>
<li>project, construction project</li>
<li>construction site, project site</li></ol>

***стройный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стройный.html>стро́йный</a> (3692)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>стро́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stróitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стройный.html>стро́йный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">strójnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)стройне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)стройне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>slender, slim, svelte
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can we date this quote?)</span>,  Alexandre Blok,  “Она <a href = vnd.unilang:стройный.html>стройна́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:высокий.html>высока́</a>  | She Is Slender and Tall | ”, in <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Please provide the book title or journal name)</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стройный.html>стройна́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:высокий.html>высока́</a><br /><a href = vnd.unilang:всегда.html>всегда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надменный.html>надме́нна</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:суровый.html>суро́ва</a>.<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:каждый.html>ка́ждый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:издалека.html>издалека́</a><br /><a href = vnd.unilang:следить.html>следи́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>не́й</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:готовый.html>гото́вый</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oná <b>strojná</b> i vysoká<br />Vsegdá nadménna i suróva.<br />Ja káždyj denʹ izdaleká<br />Sledíl za néj, na vsjó gotóvyj.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">She is <b>slender</b> and tall<br />Always haughty and severe.<br />Every day from afar<br />I watched her, ready for anything.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>well-composed, harmonious, orderly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стройный.html>стро́йном</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:порядок.html>поря́дке</a>; <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стройный.html>стро́йными</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ряд.html>ряда́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>strójnom</b> porjádke; <b>strójnymi</b> rjadámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in an orderly manner</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>harmonious <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of sounds</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стропило.html>стропи́ло</a> (22889)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">стропить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stropitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ло</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стропа.html>стро́п</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">strop</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">roof</i>)
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стропило.html>стропи́ло</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stropílo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стропило.html>стропи́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стропило.html>стропи́ла</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стропило.html>стропи́л</a></b>)
